改革初期，农民害怕被称作富裕户；今天以冒富而自豪。
Gǎigé chūqī，nóngmín hàipà bèi chēngzuò fùyùhù; jīntiān yǐ màofù ér zìháo。
In the early stages of reform, farmers were afraid to be considered well-off, but today they are proud of doing better than average.
富裕中农是较为特殊的农民阶层。
Fùyù zhōng nóng shì jiào wéi tèshū de nóngmín jiēcéng。
Wealthy middle peasants are a special kind of peasant.
裕民富国。
焦裕禄同志是全心全意为人民服务的典范
The rich landowners subjugated the peasants working the land.
Zhèxiē fùyù de dìzhǔ qiángpò nóngmín zài Dìlǐ gōngzuò。
这些富裕的地主强迫农民在地里工作。
她经济本来不宽裕，可是硬要摆谱儿。
Tā jīngjì běnlái bùkuānyù，kěshì yìng yào bǎipǔr。
Though she is not well-off, she tries to keep up appearances.
时间充裕
shíjiān chōngyù 
have ample (or plenty of) time
经济充裕
jīngjì chōngyù 
well-off
生活丰裕
shēnghuó fēngyù
live in plenty; be comfortably off
日子过得挺富裕
rìzi guò de tǐng fùyù
lead a well-to-do life
经济宽裕
jīngjì kuānyù
well-off; well-to-do
时间很宽裕。
Shíjiān hěn kuānyù。
There\'s plenty of time yet.
改革初期，农民害怕被称作富裕户；今天以冒富而自豪。
Gǎigé chūqī，nóngmín hàipà bèi chēngzuò fùyùhù; jīntiān yǐ màofù ér zìháo。
In the early stages of reform, farmers were afraid to be considered well-off, but today they are proud of doing better than average.
磨削裕量
móxiāo yùliàng
grinding tolerance
手头宽裕
shǒutóu kuānyù
be in easy circumstances; be quite well off at the moment
生活优裕
shēnɡhuó yōuyù 
be well-off; be well-to-do; live in affluence
富国裕民
fùɡuóyùmín 
make one\'s country and people rich
应付裕如
yìngfùyùrú 
handle the situation with ease; be equal to the occasion
富裕
fùyù
prosperous; well-to-do; well-off
富裕中农是较为特殊的农民阶层。
Fùyù zhōng nóng shì jiào wéi tèshū de nóngmín jiēcéng。
Wealthy middle peasants are a special kind of peasant.
父亲对儿子抱有很大希望，一心盼着他光前裕后。
Fùqīn duì érzi bàoyǒu hěndà xīwàng，yìxīn pàn zhe tā guāngqián yùhòu。
The father has great expectations for his son, hoping he can bring honor to their ancestors and prosperity to their descendants.
我们一定要找到这个村的苦根，然后从根源治理，使乡亲们尽快富裕起来！
Wǒmen yídìng yào zhǎodào zhège cūn de kǔgēn，ránhòu cóng gēnyuán zhìlǐ，shǐ xiāngqīnmen jìnkuài fùyù qǐlái！
We should find out and control the root cause of poverty in the village, and help the villagers to become better-off as soon as possible.
我也不富裕，你还是去家境宽展的老李那儿借钱吧。
Wǒ yě bú fùyù，nǐ háishi qù jiājìng kuānzhǎn de Lǎo Lǐ nàr jiè qián ba。
I am not well-off either. You\'d better borrow money from Laoli, who is comfortably off.
他们家虽然不富裕，但三口人生活得乐融融的，令人羡慕。
Tāmen jiā suīrán bú fùyù，dàn sān kǒu rén shēnghuó de lèróngróng de，lìng rén xiànmù。
Though they are not very rich, the three lived happily together, which was envied to others.
妈妈是个理家的好手，我们的生活虽不富裕但过得舒舒服服。
Māma shì gè lǐjiā de hǎoshǒu，wǒmen de shēnghuó suī bú fùyù dàn guò de shūshūfúfú。
Mother is a good house-keeper. Though we are not rich, we live a happy life.
我现在时间充裕，所以想报一个英语学习的慢班。
Wǒ xiànzài shíjiān chōngyù，suǒyǐ xiǎng bào yígè yīngyǔ xuéxí de mànbān。
Having plenty of free time, I want to enroll in a slow progress English class.
他过得并不富裕，但在买书时他向来是千金一掷。
Tā guò de bìngbú fùyù，dàn zài mǎishū shítā xiàng lái shì qiānjīn yízhì。
He doesn\'t lead a life of abundance, but he throws away money like dirt when buying books
我本是一个贫困的儒生，并不富裕。
Wǒ běn shì yígè pínkùn de rúshēng，bìngbú fùyù。
I used to be a poor Confucian scholar.
他很擅长交际，任何的场合都能应付裕如。
Tā hěn shàncháng jiāojì，rènhé de chǎnghé dōu néng yìngfù yùrú。
He is good at dealing with people and can handle any situation with ease.
你不用担心，我这个月的生活费比较余裕。
Nǐ búyòng dānxīn，wǒ zhège yuè de shēnghuófèi bǐjiào yúyù。
Don\'t worry, I have enough money to live on this month.
如果完工后还有余裕的时间，我们就去看电影吧！
Rúguǒ wángōng hòu háiyǒu yúyù de shíjiān，wǒmen jiù qù kàn diànyǐng ba！
If there is still time left after we finish the work, let\'s go to see a movie.
以前，自耕农的生活也不是我们想象的那么丰裕。
Yǐqián，zì gēng nóng de shēnghuó yě búshì wǒmen xiǎng xiàng de nàme fēngyù。
In the past, the lives of peasant landlords was not as prosperous as we assumed.
由于公司现金充裕，所以足额还上了银行贷款。
Yóuyú gōngsī xiànjīn chōngyù，suǒyǐ zúé huánshàng le yínháng dàikuǎn。
As the company has generous cash flow, it is able to pay the full price plus the bank loan.
现在小村庄的人们不但能自给自足，还把富裕的农产品卖到城市里去。
Xiànzài xiǎo cūnzhuāng de rénmen búdàn néng zìgěi zìzú，hái bǎ fùyù de nóngchǎnpǐn mài dào chéngshì lǐ qù。
Nowadays, people from small villages can not only support themselves but also sell surplus farm products to the city.
他出身于一个富裕的家庭。
Tā chūshēnyú yígè fùyùde jiātíng。
He comes from a wealthy family.
富裕地区
fùyùdìqū
prosperous area
他家很富裕。
Tājiā hěnfùyù。
His family is very well off.
不用着急，时间还很宽裕。
Búyòng zháojí，shíjiān hái hěn kuānyù.
Don\'t worry, there\'s still ample time.
绰有余裕
光前裕后
他以前也穷过，现在富裕了。
宽裕

家道小康，颇有余裕。
他在剧中扮演焦裕禄
他虽不富裕，可从不薄待亲友。
有充裕的时间

应对裕如。
家境裕如。
the affluent society
富裕社会
decent wages
充裕的工资
gracious living
优裕的生活
a year of plenty
富裕的一年
to live well
生活富裕
The Green’s are a well-heeled family.
格林一家是富裕之家。
She grew up in a moderately well-to-do family with his parents and two brothers.
她生长在一个还算富裕的家庭，家里有父母亲和两个兄弟。
He abandoned a life of wealth and ease to go to China as a missionary.
Tā fàngqì fùyù de shēnghuó，qù zhōngguó zuòle yì míng chuánjiàoshì。
他放弃富裕的生活，去中国作了一名传教士。
The problem was much greater in poor areas than in more affluent areas.
Zhège wèntí zài pínkùn dìqū yào bǐ zài fādá fùyù dìqū biǎoxiàn de yánzhòng。
这个问题在贫困地区要比在发达富裕地区表现得严重。
He was the son of a wealthy bourgeois and went to the best schools.
Tā chūshēngyú yì jiā fùyù de zhōngchǎn jiējí jiātíng，bìng jìnrùle zuìhǎo de xuéxiào。
他出生于一家富裕的中产阶级家庭，并进入了最好的学校。
We are one of the richest states on earth.
Wǒmen zǔguó shì dìqiúshàng zuì fùyù de guójiā zhī yī。
我们祖国是地球上最富裕的国家之一。
I wanted to have a flush lifestyle for as long as I could remember.
Wǒ xīwàng zài wǒ yǒu jìyìlì zhī nián dōu néng guòzhe fùyù de shēnghuó。
我希望在我有记忆力之年都能过着富裕的生活。
I got a lot of money from my wealthy uncle.
Wǒ cóng wǒ fùyù de shūshu nàlǐ dédào yí dà bǐ qián。
我从我富裕的叔叔那里得到一大笔钱。
She will be adopted into a wealthy family.
Tā jiāng bèi yí gè fùyù de jiātíng suǒ shōuyǎng。
她将被一个富裕的家庭所收养。
Our family didn\'t have much，so we lived from hand to mouth.
Wǒjiā bìng bú fùyù，shēnghuó zhǐshì zhèng yìdiǎn chī yìdiǎn。
我家并不富裕，生活只是挣一点吃一点。
They were comfortable or even wealthy by some standards.
Tāmen shēnghuó kuānyù，huòzhě ànzhào mǒuxiē biāozhǔn láishuō shènzhì hěn fùyǒu。
他们生活宽裕，或者按照某些标准来说甚至很富有。
She would have been better off if she had stuck with teaching.
Rúguǒ tā jiānchí zhíjiào de huà，tā huì guò de hěn fùyù de。
如果她坚持执教的话，她会过得很富裕的。
The rich landowners subjugated the peasants working the land.
Zhèxiē fùyù de dìzhǔ qiángpò nóngmín zài Dìlǐ gōngzuò。
这些富裕的地主强迫农民在地里工作。
The accountant embezzled thousands of dollars while working for the wealthy family.
Zhè míng kuàijì zài wèi zhège fùyù jiātíng gōngzuò qījiān dàoyòngle shù qiān měiyuán。
这名会计在为这个富裕家庭工作期间盗用了数千美元。

时间充裕
shíjiān chōngyù 
have ample (or plenty of) time
经济充裕
jīngjì chōngyù 
well-off

挪用公款
nuóyònɡ ɡōnɡkuǎn
misappropriation (or embezzlement) of public funds
法院一审作出判决，认定他挪用公款不能退还的行为构成贪污罪。
Fǎyuàn yìshěn zuòchū pànjué，rèndìngtā nuóyònggōngkuǎn bùnéng tuìhuán de xíngwéi gòuchéngtānwūzuì。
The court convicted him in first instance and confirmed that his embezzlement of public funds without means to return them constituted a crime of corruption.
你真是狗胆包天，公家的钱也敢挪用？
Nǐ zhēnshì gǒudǎn bāotiān，gōngjiā de qián yě gǎn nuóyòng？

我国法律规定，优抚金不允许被挪作他用。
